          <a class="landing-feed--story-title link link-txt" href="/culture/tech/news/a29301/christina-wallace-interview/">
           "Failure in This One Case Didn't Make Me a Failure"
          </a>
          <div class="landing-feed--story-abstract">
           <span class="abstract-text">
            Christina Wallace of BridgeUp:STEM explains how her "worst-case scenario" got her where she is today.
           </span>
           <span class="byline--author " itemprop="author" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
            By
            <a class="link link-txt byline--author-name" href="http://www.elle.com/author/5020/glynnis-macnicol/" rel="author">
             <span>

             </span>
